Heart

Will we be replaced by machines?
Machines have computational power and physical movement, but no heart. They generally perform money-maximizing tasks.
When you know about:
- 20,000 kids killed
- Tens of thousands at the brink of death by starvation, especially newborns
- Many injured children without any pain-relieving medicationโundergoing leg and hand amputations without anesthesia.
โฆthen the amount of feeling you have, and the actions you take to stop this, that are not in the direction of money maximization, is a sign of how difficult it is to replace you by a machine.
Knowing all this, if there are some people who continue living a normal, money-maximizing life, they are already machinesโjust made of flesh and bone instead of silicon and metal.
